  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_312d5e1f-cffa-457e-bef3-553d7c92fc6c'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

<span id="freeTextContainer4200162668421921522">Learning to trust a man again, yeah sure that sounds so easy. It's hard when you're a single mom with a beautiful daughter you feel you have to protect, as well as a past full of hurt and domestic violence. I barely made it out of my daughter's father's life alive. As much as I'd love to be with a guy again, he's going to have to prove that he's worth it this time.5 years </span>
  <span id="freeText4200162668421921522" style="display:none">Learning to trust a man again, yeah sure that sounds so easy. It's hard when you're a single mom with a beautiful daughter you feel you have to protect, as well as a past full of hurt and domestic violence. I barely made it out of my daughter's father's life alive. As much as I'd love to be with a guy again, he's going to have to prove that he's worth it this time.5 years of being alone would make any woman wonder what happened to the sexy side of her. My best friend thinks I'm ready to move forward, but I'm not sure yet. Meeting a few law enforcement officers who neither of us can resist physically is nice, but it won't make me change my mind. Men are dangerous. Even if he is a freaking magician in between the sheets. My heart will take a while to conquer, and that's only if he's capable of not only being a good man to me, but he has to prove he can be the man my daughter deserves as well.Arrested Heart is a standalone romance with lots of wit, love and plot twists. It's full of hot sex, hard decisions, big hearts and forever friendships. Take a peek and see if you can stop turning the pages. This is the first novel in the ARRESTED series.</span>

Contemporary fans are sure to be pleased with this book! </span>

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3181767043?book_show_action=true">Feb 08, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jewel Hart" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jewel Hart" href="/user/show/56470711-jewel-hart">Jewel Hart</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3181767043" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7746628803350097876">Author H. L. Nida dives right into the heat of the action in her exciting book, Arrested Heart, with the messy life of Lulu as a single mom and fills in the blanks as the story unfolds. You’ll be holding your breath and wondering if a stroke of serendipity will change her life for the better.<br/><br/>The story is a fast-paced 1st person account of a life gone haywire from life events, some of her making and others bad luck. From a crappy job, little help in raising her child, no decent man in sight, to t</span>
  <span id="freeText7746628803350097876" style="display:none">Author H. L. Nida dives right into the heat of the action in her exciting book, Arrested Heart, with the messy life of Lulu as a single mom and fills in the blanks as the story unfolds. You’ll be holding your breath and wondering if a stroke of serendipity will change her life for the better.<br /><br />The story is a fast-paced 1st person account of a life gone haywire from life events, some of her making and others bad luck. From a crappy job, little help in raising her child, no decent man in sight, to true friendships and plenty of steamy encounters – leaving you blushed in the end. You’re in for a ride, sometimes bumpy other times smooth as silk, but Arrested Heart is an overall stimulating and captivating story.<br /><br />The story is one that could be happening next door, to your friend, or even yourself. You’ll be drawn into the storyline like a moth to flames asking: Will the sharp-witted Lulu find happiness in a committed relationship that’s good for her daughter, too?<br /><br />The character development from Lulu to her four-year-old daughter Sveva, and supporting roles are portrayed with realistic dialog and descriptive details. You’ll feel like you’re present and privy to the lives of these characters, their mistakes, and challenges.<br /><br />The author, H.L. Nida teases and taunts you with sexual innuendos to the point you’d like for the main characters to become one in an explosive union. The romantic suspense is mind-blowing, and she doesn’t miss a beat in the realism of the hot sexual encounters.<br /><br />Arrested Heart by H.L. Nida will keep you guessing until the very end. You’ll learn the value of friendships through the main character’s eyes and the significance family plays in deciding the future for a single mom. This is an excellent read for mature audiences and is highly recommended!</span>

          </span>

<div id="review_3200591529" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3200591529" />
    <a title="J.C. Paulson" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/69013572-j-c-paulson"><img alt="J.C. Paulson" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1511564846p2/69013572.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3200591529?book_show_action=true">Feb 21, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="J.C. Paulson" class="user" itemprop="url" name="J.C. Paulson" href="/user/show/69013572-j-c-paulson">J.C. Paulson</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3200591529" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15528898148972632557">Arrested Heart stopped my own beating core.<br/>Written with intense pace from (largely) two points of view, Arrested Heart follows the rather heart-breaking life of Lulu Haan, a single mother striving to create a happy and stable life for her adorable daughter. Men have been out of the picture for some time; there’s just too much risk with a wee girl in the house. <br/>Then an unexpected shared moment of eye contact with a handsome police officer churns into much more, as Lulu rediscovers the heat in her</span>
  <span id="freeText15528898148972632557" style="display:none">Arrested Heart stopped my own beating core.<br />Written with intense pace from (largely) two points of view, Arrested Heart follows the rather heart-breaking life of Lulu Haan, a single mother striving to create a happy and stable life for her adorable daughter. Men have been out of the picture for some time; there’s just too much risk with a wee girl in the house. <br />Then an unexpected shared moment of eye contact with a handsome police officer churns into much more, as Lulu rediscovers the heat in her soul. The beautiful Liam is in similar circumstances from a hands-off-romance standpoint, although he has much more social support. <br />I won’t go on about the plot, unwilling to spoil or expose, except to say there are intense twists, high emotion and good character development. The language is thoroughly modern, with some swearing, but it sounds like your neighbour speaking . . . or even yourself.<br />It's been a long time since I couldn’t put down a book. While not high literature, all the important bits of a good read are here. Arrested Heart made me cry, steam and cheer for Lulu and Liam. <br />Lovers of sexy romance: you must try this. “Book” four hours, get comfortable, and go.</span>

          </span>

<div id="review_2896995105" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2896995105" />
    <a title="George W." class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/99885615-george-w"><img alt="George W." src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2896995105?book_show_action=true">Jul 15, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="George W." class="user" itemprop="url" name="George W." href="/user/show/99885615-george-w">George W.</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/46150327-arrested-heart">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2896995105" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17097979996493973515">I throughly enjoyed reading this novel. I found it to be an easy read and incredibly hard to put down. As you devour this book, you will feel that the characters are sitting right beside you as you turn the pages. Prior to reading Arrested Heart, I was not a fan of steamy romance novels, but H.L. Nida changed that. I so look forward to her next work. Hint: As you read this book, it would be best to have your partner or significant other close by.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3408993219" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer4254727602808374499">“Arrested heart” couldn’t have been a more appropriate title for this captivating story from H. L Nida, an American writer who loves writing romance novels. This is the first book in the Arrested series. It tells the story of Lulu, a single mum who has an abusive ex fiancé. It is really difficult for her to trust a man again, but she meets a law enforcement officer and things get complicated for her. She only has to resist temptation, that sounds easy, does it?<br/>I absolutely love Ms. Nida and her </span>
  <span id="freeText4254727602808374499" style="display:none">“Arrested heart” couldn’t have been a more appropriate title for this captivating story from H. L Nida, an American writer who loves writing romance novels. This is the first book in the Arrested series. It tells the story of Lulu, a single mum who has an abusive ex fiancé. It is really difficult for her to trust a man again, but she meets a law enforcement officer and things get complicated for her. She only has to resist temptation, that sounds easy, does it?<br />I absolutely love Ms. Nida and her writing style. She writes the hottest alpha men and the sassiest women who bring them to their knees, but she always brings a bucket load of emotions and tears right along with it. She gives you the gut punch you need to bring tears to your eyes and the feels to your belly. Thanks to her for the incredible ability to describe characters, I fell in love with each of them, but particularly with that man who was delicious!!<br />I can’t wait for more from this author. Bravo!<br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12719672213095687151">Arrested Heart by H. L. Nida is the first in her Arrested series featuring law officers who put their heart on the line. Lulu is a single mom who attracts Liam's attention. He has never dated a single mom before and struggles to say and do the right things around Lulu's daughter, Svave. Lulu has never dated anyone since the death of Svave's father, Dan. This is new ground for both of them and the mistakes and emotions escalate until the truth about Dan's death is revealed. Could these two work t</span>
  <span id="freeText12719672213095687151" style="display:none">Arrested Heart by H. L. Nida is the first in her Arrested series featuring law officers who put their heart on the line. Lulu is a single mom who attracts Liam's attention. He has never dated a single mom before and struggles to say and do the right things around Lulu's daughter, Svave. Lulu has never dated anyone since the death of Svave's father, Dan. This is new ground for both of them and the mistakes and emotions escalate until the truth about Dan's death is revealed. Could these two work through the scars and heartache?<br /><br />H. L. Nida adds much adult content in her books and Arrested Heart is no exception. She adds drama and danger that law officers have to face daily. She keeps it real, yet makes it entertaining. This novel is a great book to kick off this series. I read the second book, Arrested Minds, first and love the action she integrates. <br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7924016464045064734">Arrested Series may be one of the steamy romance stories I've really enjoyed reading for this year. How the author delved into the emotions of the character was what I really liked the most in the story. It made me feel attached to the main character and it almost felt like I was the character with all the emotions put in those scenes. I also like how independent the character is despite the difficulties in life she was experiencing. She was the epitome of a strong woman yet still just a woman w</span>
  <span id="freeText7924016464045064734" style="display:none">Arrested Series may be one of the steamy romance stories I've really enjoyed reading for this year. How the author delved into the emotions of the character was what I really liked the most in the story. It made me feel attached to the main character and it almost felt like I was the character with all the emotions put in those scenes. I also like how independent the character is despite the difficulties in life she was experiencing. She was the epitome of a strong woman yet still just a woman who is wishing for someone who'd just sincerely love and care for her. I suggest checking this out and continue on the second book as well because both are great masterpieces!!</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('S9VSthgK5PQhKCY6k1rslYJDTKAE4ioLvrgQxazWI2bJrddY2limGVHpQkC5kqjnGHuqoPw8PDs5NO72A2mQjQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('0USr8LOuRZvw0JSGKXJXUG5n1lVpahaf3oHw4es0kqxTPC4ecfwHdoAR8PwDuhMi9F8wVZG0AK9ZDQ7SRIshRw==')})
  }

This partial loads on almost every page view.  The associated React component makes
a call to SignInPromptController#get to determine if the user should see the sign in interstial.
This is determined by how many signed out pagehits the user has executed an how recently they have
last seen the insterstitial.  If the controller responds indicating the popup should appear, the
